\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
C API functions definitions for MMG3D library. 

\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Author}
Algiane Froehly (Inria/\+UBordeaux) 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxyVersion}{Version}
5 
\end{DoxyVersion}
\begin{DoxyDate}{Date}
01 2014 
\end{DoxyDate}
\begin{DoxyCopyright}{Copyright}
GNU Lesser General Public License. 
\end{DoxyCopyright}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Use the MMG3\+D\+\_\+ prefix\+: MMG5\+\_\+ prefix will became obsolete soon...
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This file contains some internal functions for the API, see the \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmg3d_8h}{mmg3d/libmmg3d.\+h}} header file for the documentation of all the usefull user\textquotesingle{}s API functions.
\end{DoxyNote}
C API for MMG3D library. 

Definition in file \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functions__3d_8c_source}{API\+\_\+functions\+\_\+3d.\+c}}.

\index{API\_functions\_3d.c@{API\_functions\_3d.c}!MMG3D\_Add\_tetrahedron@{MMG3D\_Add\_tetrahedron}}
\index{MMG3D\_Add\_tetrahedron@{MMG3D\_Add\_tetrahedron}!API\_functions\_3d.c@{API\_functions\_3d.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Add\_tetrahedron()}{MMG3D\_Add\_tetrahedron()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Add\+\_\+tetrahedron (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{v0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{v1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{v2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{v3,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ref }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Add a tetrahedron to the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em v0} & first vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em v1} & second vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em v2} & third vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em v3} & fourth vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & tetrahedron reference.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function adds a tetrahedron with vertices {\itshape v0}, {\itshape v1}, {\itshape v2}, {\itshape v3} and reference {\itshape ref} at the first available position of the mesh.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if unable to create the tetrahedron, the unit-\/offset index of the new tet if it has strictly positive volume, a negative index if it has a zero or negative volume.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+ADD\+\_\+\+TETRAHEDRON(mesh,v0,v1,v2,v3,ref,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+IN)\+:: v0,v1,v2,v3,ref~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily MMG5\+\_\+int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Add\+\_\+vertex (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{double}]{c0,  }\item[{double}]{c1,  }\item[{double}]{c2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ref }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{API\_functions\_3d.c@{API\_functions\_3d.c}!MMG3D\_Get\_edge@{MMG3D\_Get\_edge}}
\index{MMG3D\_Get\_edge@{MMG3D\_Get\_edge}!API\_functions\_3d.c@{API\_functions\_3d.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Get\_edge()}{MMG3D\_Get\_edge()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+edge (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{e0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{e1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Ridge,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the vertices and reference of the next edge in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em e0} & pointer to the first extremity of the edge. \\
\hline
{\em e1} & pointer to the second extremity of the edge. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the edge reference. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Ridge} & pointer to the flag saying if the edge is ridge. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Required} & pointer to the flag saying if the edge is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the extremities {\itshape e0}, {\itshape e1} and reference {\itshape ref} of next edge of {\itshape mesh}. It is meant to be called in a loop over all edges. When it has been called as many times as there are edges in the mesh, the internal edge counter will be reset.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+EDGE(mesh,e0,e1,ref,is\+Ridge,is\+Required,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: e0,e1~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT) \+:: ref~\newline
 INTEGER \+:: is\+Ridge,is\+Required~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+ith\+Sol\+\_\+in\+Sols\+At\+Vertices (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{int}]{i,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{s,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{pos }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get one out of several solutions at a specific vertex. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sol} & pointer to the array of solutions \\
\hline
{\em i} & position of the solution field that we want to get. \\
\hline

\hline
{\em pos} & index of the vertex on which we get the solution.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Get values of the ith field of the solution array at vertex {\itshape pos}. (pos from 1 to nb\+\_\+vertices included and {\itshape i} from 1 to {\itshape nb\+\_\+sols}). The type of solution is inferred from {\itshape sol}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+ith\+Sols\+\_\+in\+Sols\+At\+Vertices (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{int}]{i,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{s }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get one out of several solutions at all vertices in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sol} & pointer to the array of solutions \\
\hline
{\em i} & position of the solution field that we want to get. \\
\hline
{\em s} & array of the solutions at mesh vertices. The solution at vertex {\itshape k} is given by s\mbox{[}k-\/1\mbox{]} for a scalar sol, s\mbox{[}3$\ast$(k-\/1)\mbox{]}@3 for a vectorial solution and s\mbox{[}6$\ast$(k-\/1)\mbox{]}@6 for a tensor solution.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the values of the solution at the ith field of the solution array ({\itshape i} from 1 to {\itshape nb\+\_\+sols}).

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Get\_prism()}{MMG3D\_Get\_prism()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+prism (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v3,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v4,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v5,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the vertices and reference of the next prism in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em v0} & pointer to the first vertex of prism. \\
\hline
{\em v1} & pointer to the second vertex of prism. \\
\hline
{\em v2} & pointer to the third vertex of prism. \\
\hline
{\em v3} & pointer to the fourth vertex of prism. \\
\hline
{\em v4} & pointer to the fifth vertex of prism. \\
\hline
{\em v5} & pointer to the sixth vertex of prism. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the prism reference. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Required} & pointer to the flag saying if prism is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the vertices {\itshape v0}, {\itshape v1}, {\itshape v2}, {\itshape v3}, {\itshape v4}, {\itshape v5} and reference {\itshape ref} of the next prism of {\itshape mesh}. It is meant to be called in a loop over all prisms. When it has been called as many times as there are prisms, the internal loop counter will be reset.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}

 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT) \+:: ref~\newline
 INTEGER \+:: is\+Required~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\index{API\_functions\_3d.c@{API\_functions\_3d.c}!MMG3D\_Get\_tensorSol@{MMG3D\_Get\_tensorSol}}
\index{MMG3D\_Get\_tensorSol@{MMG3D\_Get\_tensorSol}!API\_functions\_3d.c@{API\_functions\_3d.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Get\_tensorSol()}{MMG3D\_Get\_tensorSol()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+tensor\+Sol (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{m11,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{m12,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{m13,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{m22,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{m23,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{m33 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the next element of a tensor solution structure. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em met} & pointer to the sol structure. \\
\hline
{\em m11} & pointer to the position (1,1) in the solution tensor. \\
\hline
{\em m12} & pointer to the position (1,2) in the solution tensor. \\
\hline
{\em m13} & pointer to the position (1,3) in the solution tensor. \\
\hline
{\em m22} & pointer to the position (2,2) in the solution tensor. \\
\hline
{\em m23} & pointer to the position (2,3) in the solution tensor. \\
\hline
{\em m33} & pointer to the position (3,3) in the solution tensor. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the next element $(m_{11},m_{12},m_{13},m_{22},m_{23},m_{33})$ of a tensor-\/valued solution field. It is meant to be called in a loop over all vertices. When it has been called as many times as there are elements in the solution, the internal loop counter will be reset.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+TENSORSOL(met,m11,m12,m13,m22,m23,m33,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: met~\newline
 REAL(KIND=8), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: m11,m12,m13,m22,m23,m33~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+tetrahedra (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{tetra,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{refs,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{are\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the vertices and reference of all tetrahedra in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline

\hline

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Get\_tetrahedron()}{MMG3D\_Get\_tetrahedron()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+tetrahedron (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v3,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the vertices and reference of the next tetrahedron in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em v0} & pointer to the first vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em v1} & pointer to the second vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em v2} & pointer to the third vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em v3} & pointer to the fourth vertex of tetrahedron. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the tetrahedron reference. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Required} & pointer to the flag saying if tetrahedron is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the vertices {\itshape v0}, {\itshape v1}, {\itshape v2}, {\itshape v3} and reference {\itshape ref} of the next tetrahedron of {\itshape mesh}. It is meant to be called in a loop over all tetrahedra. When it has been called as many times as there are tetrahedra, the internal loop counter will be reset.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+TETRAHEDRON(mesh,v0,v1,v2,v3,ref,is\+Required,\&~\newline

 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT) \+:: ref~\newline
 INTEGER \+:: is\+Required~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{API__functions__3d_8c_a487e316efdcbee4a70d8e7bf13bfc0bb}\label{API__functions__3d_8c_a487e316efdcbee4a70d8e7bf13bfc0bb}} 
\index{API\_functions\_3d.c@{API\_functions\_3d.c}!MMG3D\_Get\_tetrahedronQuality@{MMG3D\_Get\_tetrahedronQuality}}
\index{MMG3D\_Get\_tetrahedronQuality@{MMG3D\_Get\_tetrahedronQuality}!API\_functions\_3d.c@{API\_functions\_3d.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Get\_tetrahedronQuality()}{MMG3D\_Get\_tetrahedronQuality()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily double MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+tetrahedron\+Quality (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{k }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the quality measure of a single tetrahedron in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer to the metric structure (may be NULL for an isotropic metric). \\
\hline
{\em k} & index of the tetrahedron for which we want to get the quality (from 1 to the number of tetrahedra included) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the computed quality or 0 in case of failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function returns the quality measure of tetrahedron {\itshape k}. Quality values range from 0 (degenerate) to 1 (best attainable). The function returns 0 if the tetrahedron is flat or has a negative volume, and also if {\itshape k} is out of range. In the latter case it will also print a diagnostic message to standard output.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+TETRAHEDRONQUALITY(mesh,met,k,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh,met~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+IN)\+:: k~\newline
 REAL(KIND=8), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Get\_triangle()}{MMG3D\_Get\_triangle()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+triangle (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v0,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{v2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the vertices and reference of the next triangle in the mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em v0} & pointer to the first vertex of triangle. \\
\hline
{\em v1} & pointer to the second vertex of triangle. \\
\hline
{\em v2} & pointer to the third vertex of triangle. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the triangle reference. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Required} & pointer to the flag saying if triangle is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the vertices {\itshape v0}, {\itshape v1}, {\itshape v2}, and reference {\itshape ref} of the next triangle of {\itshape mesh}. It is meant to be called in a loop over all triangles. When it has been called as many times as there are triangles, the internal loop counter will be reset.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+TRIANGLE(mesh,v0,v1,v2,ref,is\+Required,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: v0,v1,v2~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT) \+:: ref~\newline
 INTEGER \+:: is\+Required~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Get\_vectorSol()}{MMG3D\_Get\_vectorSol()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+vector\+Sol (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{vx,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{vy,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{vz }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the next element of a vector solution structure. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em met} & pointer to the sol structure. \\
\hline
{\em vx} & x value of the vectorial solution. \\
\hline
{\em vy} & y value of the vectorial solution. \\
\hline
{\em vz} & z value of the vectorial solution. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the next vector-\/valued element $(v_x,v_y,vz)$ of the solution. It is meant to be called in a loop over all elements. When it has been called as many times as there are elements in the solution, the internal loop counter will be reset.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Get\_vertex()}{MMG3D\_Get\_vertex()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+vertex (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{c0,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{c1,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{c2,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{ref,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Corner,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{is\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the coordinates {\itshape c0}, {\itshape c1},{\itshape c2} and reference {\itshape ref} of the next vertex of {\itshape mesh}. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em c0} & pointer to the coordinate of the vertex along the first dimension. \\
\hline
{\em c1} & pointer to the coordinate of the vertex along the second dimension. \\
\hline
{\em c2} & pointer to the coordinate of the vertex along the third dimension. \\
\hline
{\em ref} & pointer to the vertex reference. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Corner} & pointer to the flag saying if vertex is corner. \\
\hline
{\em is\+Required} & pointer to the flag saying if vertex is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function retrieves the coordinates {\itshape c0}, {\itshape c1},{\itshape c2} and reference {\itshape ref} of the next vertex of a mesh. It is meant to be used in a loop over all vertices. When this function has been called as many times as there are vertices, the internal loop counter will be reset. To obtain data for a specific vertex, the \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functions__3d_8c_a04f98ce8620e83b2606115bfdf531b6c}{MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+By\+Idx\+\_\+vertex}} function can be used instead.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+VERTEX(mesh,c0,c1,c2,ref,is\+Corner,is\+Required, \&~\newline
 retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh~\newline
 REAL(KIND=8), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: c0,c1,c2~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT) \+:: ref~\newline
 INTEGER \+:: is\+Corner,is\+Required~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
For the MMG3\+D\+\_\+mmg3dlib function, you need to call the \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functions__3d_8c_a00ec28ed5d8e31f7c12cc1749403085c}{MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh}} function with the following arguments \+: MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh, MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Met \+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Met, \&your\+\_\+metric,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

For the MMG3\+D\+\_\+mmg3dls function, you need to call the \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functions__3d_8c_a00ec28ed5d8e31f7c12cc1749403085c}{MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh}} function with the following arguments \+: MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh, MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Ls, \&your\+\_\+level\+\_\+set,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

For the MMG3\+D\+\_\+mmg3dmov function, you must call \+: MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh, \+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Met,\&empty\+\_\+metric,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Disp, \&your\+\_\+displacement, \+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

Here, {\itshape your\+\_\+mesh} is a \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}, {\itshape your\+\_\+metric} {\itshape your\+\_\+level\+\_\+set} and {\itshape your\+\_\+displacement} are \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 on success, 0 on failure
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function allocates and initializes MMG structures. All structures of types MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh and MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol that will be given as arguments to Mmg functions must be initialized with this function.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
No fortran interface to allow variadic arguments.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
detected bugs\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item some vertices along open boundaries end up with a normal (while they should not) 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyWarning}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+ls\+Base\+Reference (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{br }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set a new level-\/set base reference. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer to the sol structure. \\
\hline
{\em br} & new level-\/set base reference. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Set a new level-\/set base reference of ref {\itshape br} in LS discretization mode. Base references are boundary conditions to which implicit domains can be attached. All implicit volumes that are not attached to listed base references are deleted as spurious volumes by the {\itshape rmc} option.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}

 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+mesh\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{np,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ne,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{nprism,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{nt,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{nquad,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{na }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the number of vertices, tetrahedra, prisms, triangles, quadrilaterals, and edges of a mesh. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline

\hline

\hline

\hline
{\em nt} & number of triangles. \\
\hline

\hline

\hline

\end{DoxyReturn}
This function sets the number of vertices, tetrahedra, prisms, triangles, quadrilaterals and edges of the mesh and allocates the associated arrays. If called again, it will reset the whole mesh to reallocate it at the new size

\index{API\_functions\_3d.c@{API\_functions\_3d.c}!MMG3D\_Set\_multiMat@{MMG3D\_Set\_multiMat}}
\index{MMG3D\_Set\_multiMat@{MMG3D\_Set\_multiMat}!API\_functions\_3d.c@{API\_functions\_3d.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Set\_multiMat()}{MMG3D\_Set\_multiMat()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+multi\+Mat (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ref,  }\item[{int}]{split,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{rmin,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{rplus }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the reference mapping for the elements of reference {\itshape ref} in level-\/set discretization mode. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer to the sol structure \\
\hline
{\em ref} & input tetrahedron reference \\
\hline
{\em split} & MMG5\+\_\+\+MMAT\+\_\+\+No\+Split if the entity must not be splitted, MMG5\+\_\+\+MMAT\+\_\+\+Split otherwise \\
\hline
{\em rmin} & reference for the negative side after LS discretization \\
\hline
{\em rplus} & reference for the positive side after LS discretization \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+SET\+\_\+\+MULTIMAT(mesh,sol,ref,split,rmin,rplus,retval)~\newline
 MMG5\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+PTR\+\_\+T,INTENT(\+INOUT) \+:: mesh,sol~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+IN) \+:: split~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+IN)\+:: ref,rmin,rplus~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}
With this function you can determine which references will be given to the tetrahedra on both sides of the level set, after discretization. Negative and positive here refer to volumes where the function is smaller or larger, respectively, than the isovalue of the level set. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

{\em quads} & pointer to the array of the quads vertices Vertices of the $i^{th}$ quadra are stored in quads\mbox{[}(i-\/1)$\ast$3\mbox{]}@3. \\
\hline
{\em refs} & pointer to the array of the quadrilateral references. refs\mbox{[}i-\/1\mbox{]} is the ref of the $i^{th}$ quadra. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: (commentated in order to allow to pass \%val(0) instead of the refs array)
\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Set\_vertices()}{MMG3D\_Set\_vertices()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+vertices (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{vertices,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{refs }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set all vertex coordinates and references in a mesh structure. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer to the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em vertices} & array of vertex coordinates in the order $[x_1, y_1, z_1, x_2, \ldots, z_N]$ where $N$ is the number of vertices in the mesh. \\
\hline
{\em refs} & array of vertex references. The reference of vertex $i$ is stored in refs\mbox{[} $i-1$\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function sets the coordinates and references of all vertices in a mesh structure. The number of vertices in the mesh must have been set before.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: (commentated in order to allow to pass \%val(0) instead of the refs array)
\end{DoxyRemark}

! INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
! END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}
